if (!is_file('index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: index.php');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index.php') != '3a3eaaa0a6ad6580598ea8f695f895e7bb0b046c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '3a3eaaa0a6ad6580598ea8f695f895e7bb0b046c') {
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '1f5dab82b11fe2ec111551da26d388fb738cf410') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '3a3eaaa0a6ad6580598ea8f695f895e7bb0b046c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index.php');
		}
	}
}

			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus.css')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus.css', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.css') !== '40787b15171d205dc5e099c6ca0a97b1e7580830') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus.css');
		}
	}
}

	}

			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== '823223eda6f564f72e41ae200eafcb2aa63030ad') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/setup.css')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/setup.css');
	writefile_11();
	if (!is_file('setup/setup.css')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/setup.css');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/setup.css') != 'ceac036c7349594a6cd66e54f7a3b5489eb739a5') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/setup.css');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/setup.css', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/setup.css');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.css') !== 'ceac036c7349594a6cd66e54f7a3b5489eb739a5') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.css') !== 'c56e2d2fe6a537bda634c9a4f722925f6c5b5310') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/setup.css');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/setup.css');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/setup.css')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/setup.css', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.css') !== 'ceac036c7349594a6cd66e54f7a3b5489eb739a5') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/setup.css');
		}
	}
}
